Required conditions: Conditions are required for kubelet to work\n// properly. If any required condition is unmet, the node will be not ready.\n// The required conditions include:\n//   * RuntimeReady: RuntimeReady means the runtime is up and ready to accept\n//   basic containers e.g. container only needs host network.\n//   * NetworkReady: NetworkReady means the runtime network is up and ready to\n//   accept containers which require container network.\n// 2. Optional conditions: Conditions are informative to the user, but kubelet\n// will not rely on. Since condition type is an arbitrary string, all conditions\n// not required are optional. These conditions will be exposed to users to help\n// them understand the status of the system.\nmessage RuntimeCondition {\n    // Type of runtime condition.\n    string type = 1;\n    // Status of the condition, one of true/false. Default: false.\n    bool status = 2;\n    // Brief CamelCase string containing reason for the condition's last transition.\n    string reason = 3;\n    // Human-readable message indicating details about last transition.\n    string message = 4;\n}\n\n// RuntimeStatus is information about the current status of the runtime.\nmessage RuntimeStatus {\n    // List of current observed runtime conditions.\n    repeated RuntimeCondition conditions = 1;\n}\n\nmessage StatusRequest {\n    // Verbose indicates whether to return extra information about the runtime.\n    bool verbose = 1;\n}\n\n// RuntimeHandlerFeatures is a set of features implemented by the runtime handler.\nmessage RuntimeHandlerFeatures {\n    // recursive_read_only_mounts is set to true if the runtime handler supports\n    // recursive read-only mounts.\n    // For runc-compatible runtimes, availability of this feature can be detected by checking whether\n    // the Linux kernel version is >= 5.12, and,  `runc features | jq .mountOptions` contains \"rro\".\n    bool recursive_read_only_mounts = 1;\n\n    // user_namespaces is set to true if the runtime handler supports user namespaces as implemented\n    // in Kubernetes. This means support for both, user namespaces and idmap mounts.\n    bool user_namespaces = 2;\n}\n\nmessage RuntimeHandler {\n    // Name must be unique in StatusResponse.\n    // An empty string denotes the default handler.\n    string name = 1;\n    // Supported features.\n    RuntimeHandlerFeatures features = 2;\n}\n\n// RuntimeFeatures describes the set of features implemented by the CRI implementation.\n// The features contained in the RuntimeFeatures should depend only on the cri implementation\n// independent of runtime handlers.\nmessage RuntimeFeatures {\n    // supplemental_groups_policy is set to true if the runtime supports SupplementalGroupsPolicy and ContainerUser.\n    bool supplemental_groups_policy = 1;\n}\n\nmessage StatusResponse {\n    // Status of the Runtime.\n    RuntimeStatus status = 1;\n    // Info is extra information of the Runtime. The key could be arbitrary string, and\n    // value should be in json format. The information could include anything useful for\n    // debug, e.g. plugins used by the container runtime.\n    // It should only be returned non-empty when Verbose is true.\n    map<string, string> info = 2;\n    // Runtime handlers.\n    repeated RuntimeHandler runtime_handlers = 3;\n    // features describes the set of features implemented by the CRI implementation.\n    // This field is supposed to propagate to NodeFeatures in Kubernetes API.\n    RuntimeFeatures features = 4;\n}\n\nmessage ImageFsInfoRequest {}\n\n// UInt64Value is the wrapper of uint64.\nmessage UInt64Value {\n    // The value.\n    uint64 value = 1;\n}\n\n// FilesystemIdentifier uniquely identify the filesystem.\nmessage FilesystemIdentifier{\n    // Mountpoint of a filesystem.\n    string mountpoint = 1;\n}\n\n// FilesystemUsage provides the filesystem usage information.\nmessage FilesystemUsage {\n    // Timestamp in nanoseconds at which the information were collected. Must be > 0.\n    int64 timestamp = 1;\n    // The unique identifier of the filesystem.\n    FilesystemIdentifier fs_id = 2;\n    // UsedBytes represents the bytes used for images on the filesystem.\n    // This may differ from the total bytes used on the filesystem and may not\n    // equal CapacityBytes - AvailableBytes.\n    UInt64Value used_bytes = 3;\n    // InodesUsed represents the inodes used by the images.\n    // This may not equal InodesCapacity - InodesAvailable because the underlying\n    // filesystem may also be used for purposes other than storing images.\n    UInt64Value inodes_used = 4;\n}\n\n// WindowsFilesystemUsage provides the filesystem usage information specific to Windows.\nmessage WindowsFilesystemUsage {\n    // Timestamp in nanoseconds at which the information were collected. Must be > 0.\n    int64 timestamp = 1;\n    // The unique identifier of the filesystem.\n    FilesystemIdentifier fs_id = 2;\n    // UsedBytes represents the bytes used for images on the filesystem.\n    // This may differ from the total bytes used on the filesystem and may not\n    // equal CapacityBytes - AvailableBytes.\n    UInt64Value used_bytes = 3;\n}\n\nmessage ImageFsInfoResponse {\n    // Information of image filesystem(s).\n    repeated FilesystemUsage image_filesystems = 1;\n    // Information of container filesystem(s).\n    // This is an optional field, may be used for example if container and image\n    // storage are separated.\n    // Default will be to return this as empty.\n    repeated FilesystemUsage container_filesystems = 2;\n}\n\nmessage ContainerStatsRequest{\n    // ID of the container for which to retrieve stats.\n    string container_id = 1;\n}\n\nmessage ContainerStatsResponse {\n    // Stats of the container.\n    ContainerStats stats = 1;\n}\n\nmessage ListContainerStatsRequest{\n    // Filter for the list request.\n    ContainerStatsFilter filter = 1;\n}\n\n// ContainerStatsFilter is used to filter containers.\n// All those fields are combined with 'AND'\nmessage ContainerStatsFilter {\n    // ID of the container.\n    string id = 1;\n    // ID of the PodSandbox.\n    string pod_sandbox_id = 2;\n    // LabelSelector to select matches.\n    // Only api.MatchLabels is supported for now and the requirements\n    // are ANDed. MatchExpressions is not supported yet.\n    map<string, string> label_selector = 3;\n}\n\nmessage ListContainerStatsResponse {\n    // Stats of the container.\n    repeated ContainerStats stats = 1;\n}\n\n// ContainerAttributes provides basic information of the container.\nmessage ContainerAttributes {\n    // ID of the container.\n    string id = 1;\n    // Metadata of the container.\n    ContainerMetadata metadata = 2;\n    // Key-value pairs that may be used to scope and select individual resources.\n    map<string,string> labels = 3;\n    // Unstructured key-value map holding arbitrary metadata.\n    // Annotations MUST NOT be altered by the runtime; the value of this field\n    // MUST be identical to that of the corresponding ContainerConfig used to\n    // instantiate the Container this status represents.\n    map<string,string> annotations = 4;\n}\n\n// ContainerStats provides the resource usage statistics for a container.\nmessage ContainerStats {\n    // Information of the container.\n    ContainerAttributes attributes = 1;\n    // CPU usage gathered from the container.\n    CpuUsage cpu = 2;\n    // Memory usage gathered from the container.\n    MemoryUsage memory = 3;\n    // Usage of the writable layer.\n    FilesystemUsage writable_layer = 4;\n    // Swap usage gathered from the container.\n    SwapUsage swap = 5;\n    // IO usage gathered from the container.\n    IoUsage io = 6;\n}\n\n// WindowsContainerStats provides the resource usage statistics for a container specific for Windows\nmessage WindowsContainerStats {\n    // Information of the container.\n    ContainerAttributes attributes = 1;\n    // CPU usage gathered from the container.\n    WindowsCpuUsage cpu = 2;\n    // Memory usage gathered from the container.\n    WindowsMemoryUsage memory = 3;\n    // Usage of the writable layer.\n    WindowsFilesystemUsage writable_layer = 4;\n}\n\n// PSI statistics for an individual resource.\nmessage PsiStats {\n\t// PSI data for all tasks in the cgroup.\n\tPsiData Full = 1;\n\t// PSI data for some tasks in the cgroup.\n\tPsiData Some = 2;\n}\n\n// PSI data for an individual resource.\nmessage PsiData {\n\t// Total time duration for tasks in the cgroup have waited due to congestion.\n\t// Unit: nanoseconds.\n\tuint64 Total = 1;\n\t// The average (in %) tasks have waited due to congestion over a 10 second window.\n\tdouble Avg10 = 2;\n\t// The average (in %) tasks have waited due to congestion over a 60 second window.\n\tdouble Avg60 = 3;\n\t// The average (in %) tasks have waited due to congestion over a 300 second window.\n\tdouble Avg300 = 4;\n}\n\n// CpuUsage provides the CPU usage information.\nmessage CpuUsage {\n    // Timestamp in nanoseconds at which the information were collected. Must be > 0.\n    int64 timestamp = 1;\n    // Cumulative CPU usage (sum across all cores) since object creation.\n    UInt64Value usage_core_nano_seconds = 2;\n    // Total CPU usage (sum of all cores) averaged over the sample window.\n    // The \"core\" unit can be interpreted as CPU core-nanoseconds per second.\n    UInt64Value usage_nano_cores = 3;\n    // CPU PSI statistics.\n    PsiStats psi = 4;\n}\n\n// WindowsCpuUsage provides the CPU usage information specific to Windows\nmessage WindowsCpuUsage {\n    // Timestamp in nanoseconds at which the information were collected. Must be > 0.\n    int64 timestamp = 1;\n    // Cumulative CPU usage (sum across all cores) since object creation.\n    UInt64Value usage_core_nano_seconds = 2;\n    // Total CPU usage (sum of all cores) averaged over the sample window.\n    // The \"core\" unit can be interpreted as CPU core-nanoseconds per second.\n    UInt64Value usage_nano_cores = 3;\n}\n\n// MemoryUsage provides the memory usage information.\nmessage MemoryUsage {\n    // Timestamp in nanoseconds at which the information were collected. Must be > 0.\n    int64 timestamp = 1;\n    // The amount of working set memory in bytes.\n    UInt64Value working_set_bytes = 2;\n    // Available memory for use. This is defined as the memory limit - workingSetBytes.\n    UInt64Value available_bytes = 3;\n    // Total memory in use. This includes all memory regardless of when it was accessed.\n    UInt64Value usage_bytes = 4;\n    // The amount of anonymous and swap cache memory (includes transparent hugepages).\n    UInt64Value rss_bytes = 5;\n    // Cumulative number of minor page faults.\n    UInt64Value page_faults = 6;\n    // Cumulative number of major page faults.\n    UInt64Value major_page_faults = 7;\n    // Memory PSI statistics.\n    PsiStats psi = 8;\n}\n\nmessage IoUsage {\n    // Timestamp in nanoseconds at which the information were collected. Must be > 0.\n    int64 timestamp = 1;\n    // IO PSI statistics.\n    PsiStats psi = 2;\n}\n\nmessage SwapUsage {\n    // Timestamp in nanoseconds at which the information were collected. Must be > 0.\n    int64 timestamp = 1;\n    // Available swap for use. This is defined as the swap limit - swapUsageBytes.\n    UInt64Value swap_available_bytes = 2;\n    // Total memory in use. `/ccb_crossrepo/src/kubernetes/staging/src/k8s.io/cri-api/pkg/apis/runtime/v1/`\n- **Key Files**:\n  - `api.proto` - Protocol Buffer definition of CRI gRPC services\n  - `api_grpc.pb.go` - Generated methods)\n\nManages pod sandboxes, containers, and container execution.\n\n**Pod Sandbox Management (6 methods):**\n```\n- rpc Version(VersionRequest) returns (VersionResponse)\n- rpc returns (RemovePodSandboxResponse)\n- rpc PodSandboxStatus(PodSandboxStatusRequest) returns (PodSandboxStatusResponse)\n- rpc ListPodSandbox(ListPodSandboxRequest) returns (ListPodSandboxResponse)\n```\n\n**Container Management (8 methods):**\n```\n- rpc CreateContainer(CreateContainerRequest) returns (CreateContainerResponse)\n- rpc StartContainer(StartContainerRequest) returns (StartContainerResponse)\n- rpc StopContainer(StopContainerRequest) returns (StopContainerResponse)\n- rpc RemoveContainer(RemoveContainerRequest) returns (RemoveContainerResponse)\n- rpc ListContainers(ListContainersRequest) returns (ListContainersResponse)\n- rpc ContainerStatus(ContainerStatusRequest) returns (ContainerStatusResponse)\n- rpc UpdateContainerResources(UpdateContainerResourcesRequest) returns (UpdateContainerResourcesResponse)\n- rpc ReopenContainerLog(ReopenContainerLogRequest) returns (ReopenContainerLogResponse)\n```\n\n**Container Execution (4 methods):**\n```\n- rpc ExecSync(ExecSyncRequest) returns (ExecSyncResponse)\n- rpc Exec(ExecRequest) returns (ExecResponse)\n- rpc Attach(AttachRequest) returns (AttachResponse)\n- rpc PortForward(PortForwardRequest) returns (PortForwardResponse)\n```\n\n**Stats & Monitoring (6 methods):**\n```\n- rpc PodSandboxStats(PodSandboxStatsRequest) returns (PodSandboxStatsResponse)\n- rpc ListPodSandboxStats(ListPodSandboxStatsRequest) returns (ListPodSandboxStatsResponse)\n- rpc UpdateRuntimeConfig(UpdateRuntimeConfigRequest) returns (UpdateRuntimeConfigResponse)\n- rpc Status(StatusRequest) returns (StatusResponse)\n```\n\n**Advanced Features (2 methods):**\n```\n- rpc CheckpointContainer(CheckpointContainerRequest) returns (CheckpointContainerResponse)\n- rpc GetContainerEvents(GetEventsRequest) returns (stream ContainerEventResponse)\n```\n\n**Metrics & (ListPodSandboxMetricsResponse)\n- rpc RuntimeConfig(RuntimeConfigRequest) returns (RuntimeConfigResponse)\n- rpc UpdatePodSandboxResources(UpdatePodSandboxResourcesRequest) returns (UpdatePodSandboxResourcesResponse)\n```\n\n#### 2. **ImageService** (5 RPC methods)\n\nManages container images.\n\n```\n- rpc ListImages(ListImagesRequest) returns (ListImagesResponse)\n- rpc ImageStatus(ImageStatusRequest) returns (ImageStatusResponse)\n- rpc PullImage(PullImageRequest) returns (PullImageResponse)\n- rpc RemoveImage(RemoveImageRequest) returns (RemoveImageResponse)\n- rpc ImageFsInfo(ImageFsInfoRequest) returns (ImageFsInfoResponse)\n```\n\n### Generated Code Structure\n\n**File**: `api_grpc.pb.go`\n\nContains:\n- **Service Constants**: Full method names (e.g., `/runtime.v1.RuntimeService/RunPodSandbox`)\n- **Client Interfaces**: `RuntimeServiceClient` and `ImageServiceClient`\n- **Server Interfaces**: `RuntimeServiceServer` and `ImageServiceServer`\n- **Server Registration Functions**: `RegisterRuntimeServiceServer()`, `RegisterImageServiceServer()`\n\n**Example Interface Contract**:\n```go\ntype RuntimeServiceServer interface {\n    Version(context.Context, *VersionRequest) (*VersionResponse, error)\n    RunPodSandbox(context.Context, *RunPodSandboxRequest) (*RunPodSandboxResponse, error)\n    StopPodSandbox(context.Context, *StopPodSandboxRequest) (*StopPodSandboxResponse, error)\n    RemovePodSandbox(context.Context, *RemovePodSandboxRequest) (*RemovePodSandboxResponse, error)\n    // ... 23 more methods\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## Part 2: Kubernetes Vendoring of CRI Types\n\n### Dependency Chain\n\n**Kubernetes go.mod**:\n```\nk8s.io/cri-api v0.0.0\n    => ./staging/src/k8s.io/cri-api\n```\n\nThis is a **replace directive**, meaning:\n- Kubernetes maintains CRI API definitions as a staging area\n- The staging source is the canonical location for CRI API definitions\n- Kubernetes can update CRI APIs in lockstep with kubelet changes\n\n**File Structure**:\n```\nstaging/src/k8s.io/cri-api/\n├── pkg/\n│   ├── apis/\n│   │   └── runtime/\n│   │       └── v1/\n│   │           ├── api.proto          # Source definitions\n│   │           ├── api.pb.go          # Generated message types\n│   │           ├── api_grpc.pb.go     # Generated gRPC code\n│   │           └── constants.go       # CRI constants\n│   └── errors/\n│       └── errors.go                  # CRI error definitions\n```\n\n**Key Contract Elements**:\n\n1. **Message Types**: Fully defined in `api.pb.go` with Go struct definitions matching protobuf messages\n2. **gRPC Interfaces**: Defined in `api_grpc.pb.go`\n3. **Constants**:\n   - Error codes (e.g., `RuntimeUnsupported`, `InvalidArgument`)\n   - Log paths, container state constants\n   - Named in `/ccb_crossrepo/src/kubernetes/staging/src/k8s.io/cri-api/pkg/apis/runtime/v1/constants.go`\n\n---\n\n## Part 3: Containerd's CRI Implementation\n\n### Plugin Architecture\n\n**Location**: `/ccb_crossrepo/src/containerd/plugins/cri/`\n\nContainerd implements CRI as a **gRPC plugin** with two main components:\n\n#### 3.1 Plugin Initialization\n\n**File**: `/ccb_crossrepo/src/containerd/plugins/cri/cri.go`\n\n**Plugin Registration**:\n```go\nregistry.Register(&plugin.Registration{\n    Type: plugins.GRPCPlugin,      // Registers as gRPC plugin\n    ID:   \"cri\",\n    Requires: []plugin.Type{\n        plugins.CRIServicePlugin,         // Runtime service dependency\n        plugins.CRIServicePlugin,         // Image service dependency\n        plugins.PodSandboxPlugin,         // Sandbox controller\n        plugins.SandboxControllerPlugin,  // Sandbox management\n        plugins.NRIApiPlugin,             // NRI integration\n        plugins.EventPlugin,              // Event system\n        plugins.ServicePlugin,            // Service registry\n        plugins.LeasePlugin,              // Resource leases\n        plugins.SandboxStorePlugin,       // Sandbox persistence\n        plugins.TransferPlugin,           // Content transfer\n        plugins.WarningPlugin,            // Warning service\n    },\n})\n```\n\n**Initialization Flow**:\n1. Plugin loads runtime service plugin (\"runtime\")\n2. Plugin loads image service plugin (\"images\")\n3. Creates containerd client with in-memory services\n4. Creates CRI gRPC server by calling `server.NewCRIService()`\n5. Wraps server in `criGRPCServer` which implements both `RuntimeServiceServer` and `ImageServiceServer`\n6. Registers servers with gRPC: `runtime.RegisterRuntimeServiceServer()` and `runtime.RegisterImageServiceServer()`\n\n**Key Wrapper** (lines 163-174):\n```go\ntype criGRPCServer struct {\n    runtime.RuntimeServiceServer    // Embedded interface\n    runtime.ImageServiceServer      // Embedded interface\n    io.Closer\n    initializer\n}\n\nfunc (c *criGRPCServer) register(s *grpc.Server) error {\n    instrumented := instrument.NewService(c)\n    runtime.RegisterRuntimeServiceServer(s, instrumented)\n    runtime.RegisterImageServiceServer(s, instrumented)\n    return nil\n}\n```\n\n#### 3.2 Runtime Service Implementation\n\n**Location**: `/ccb_crossrepo/src/containerd/internal/cri/server/`\n\n**Core Service Structure** (`service.go`):\n```go\ntype criService struct {\n    runtime.UnimplementedRuntimeServiceServer\n    runtime.UnimplementedImageServiceServer\n\n    // State management\n    sandboxStore *sandboxstore.Store\n    containerStore *containerstore.Store\n\n    // Clients and plugins\n    client *containerd.Client\n    netPlugin map[string]cni.CNI\n\n    // Execution\n    streamServer streaming.Server\n    eventMonitor *events.EventMonitor\n}\n```\n\n**Inheritance**:\n- Embeds `runtime.UnimplementedRuntimeServiceServer` (from generated protobuf code)\n- This provides stub implementations of all methods\n- Each method is overridden with actual implementation\n\n### Implementation Details by Method Category\n\n#### Pod Sandbox Operations\n\n**RunPodSandbox** (`sandbox_run.go:53`)\n```go\nfunc (c *criService) RunPodSandbox(ctx context.Context, r *runtime.RunPodSandboxRequest)\n    (_ *runtime.RunPodSandboxResponse, retErr error)\n```\n**Flow**:\n1. Generate unique sandbox ID and name\n2. Reserve sandbox name to prevent conflicts\n3. Create containerd lease for resource tracking\n4. Load OCI runtime configuration from request\n5. Create sandbox info with runtime metadata\n6. Call platform-specific implementation (`sandbox_run_linux.go`, `sandbox_run_windows.go`, etc.)\n7. Return sandbox ID in response\n\n**Key Dependencies**:\n- `sandboxNameIndex` - Name uniqueness enforcement\n- `sandboxStore` - Persistent storage of sandbox metadata\n- Lease service - Resource lifecycle management\n- Platform-specific sandbox operations\n\n**StopPodSandbox** (`sandbox_stop.go:35`)\n```go\nfunc (c *criService) StopPodSandbox(ctx context.Context, r *runtime.StopPodSandboxRequest)\n    (*runtime.StopPodSandboxResponse, error)\n```\n**Idempotency**: Returns success even if sandbox already stopped (CRI requirement)\n\n**RemovePodSandbox** (`sandbox_remove.go`)\n```\nRemoves sandbox and all associated resources\n```\n\n**PodSandboxStatus** (`sandbox_status.go`)\n```\nReturns detailed sandbox status including network namespace, IPs, and container states\n```\n\n**ListPodSandbox** (`sandbox_list.go`)\n```\nLists sandboxes with optional filtering\n```\n\n#### Container Operations\n\n**CreateContainer** (`container_create.go:60`)\n```go\nfunc (c *criService) CreateContainer(ctx context.Context, r *runtime.CreateContainerRequest)\n    (_ *runtime.CreateContainerResponse, retErr error)\n```\n**Flow**:\n1. Validate sandbox exists and is running\n2. Generate unique container ID and name\n3. Load container configuration and image\n4. Build OCI runtime specification from Kubernetes config\n5. Generate containerd container spec\n6. Store container metadata\n7. Return container ID\n\n**Spec Generation**:\n- Converts Kubernetes container config to OCI runtime spec\n- Handles platform-specific options (Linux: seccomp, AppArmor, SELinux; Windows: HyperV options)\n- Applies resource limits, environment variables, mounts\n- Configures logging, working directory, entrypoint\n\n**StartContainer** (`container_start.go`)\n```\nStarts the container task using OCI runtime\n```\n\n**StopContainer** (`container_stop.go`)\n```\nStops container with grace period before forcible termination\n```\n\n**RemoveContainer** (`container_remove.go`)\n```\nRemoves container and releases all resources\n```\n\n**ContainerStatus** (`container_status.go`)\n```\nReturns container status including state, created time, exit code\n```\n\n#### Container Execution\n\n**ExecSync** (`container_execsync.go`)\n```\nSynchronous command execution in container\n```\n\n**Exec** (`container_exec.go`)\n```\nPrepares streaming endpoint for interactive command execution\n```\n\n**Attach** (`container_attach.go`)\n```\nAttaches to container's stdio streams\n```\n\n**PortForward** (`sandbox_portforward.go`)\n```\nForwards ports between host and sandbox\n```\n\n#### Stats and Metrics\n\n**ContainerStats** (`container_stats.go`)\n```\nReturns container resource usage statistics\n```\n\n**ListContainerStats** (`container_stats_list.go`)\n```\nLists stats for all containers with filtering\n```\n\n**PodSandboxStats** (`sandbox_stats.go`)\n```\nReturns aggregate sandbox statistics\n```\n\n**ListPodSandboxMetrics** (`list_pod_sandbox_metrics_linux.go`)\n```\nLists metrics for sandboxes (Linux-specific)\n```\n\n#### Configuration and Runtime\n\n**Status** (`status.go`)\n```\nReturns overall runtime status\n```\n\n**UpdateRuntimeConfig** (`update_runtime_config.go`)\n```\nUpdates runtime configuration dynamically\n```\n\n**RuntimeConfig** (`runtime_config.go`)\n```\nReturns current runtime configuration\n```\n\n### Image Service Implementation\n\n**Location**: `/ccb_crossrepo/src/containerd/internal/cri/server/images/`\n\n**Service Structure** (`service.go`):\n```go\ntype imageService struct {\n    runtime.UnimplementedImageServiceServer\n\n    // Image storage\n    imageStore imagestore.Store\n\n    // Snapshot management\n    snapshotter string\n\n    // Client references\n    client *containerd.Client\n}\n```\n\n**Key Methods**:\n- **ListImages** (`image_list.go`) - Lists available images\n- **ImageStatus** (`image_status.go`) - Returns image metadata and digest\n- **PullImage** (`image_pull.go`) - Downloads image from registry with authentication\n- **RemoveImage** (`image_remove.go`) - Deletes image and clean up resources\n- **ImageFsInfo** (`imagefs_info.go`) - Returns filesystem usage for image storage\n\n### Instrumentation & Middleware\n\n**File**: `/ccb_crossrepo/src/containerd/internal/cri/instrument/`\n\nAll RPC calls are wrapped with instrumentation middleware that:\n- Adds distributed tracing spans\n- Records metrics (latency, error rates)\n- Logs method calls at appropriate verbosity levels\n\n**Wrapping Pattern** (from `cri.go:171`):\n```go\ninstrumented := instrument.NewService(c)\nruntime.RegisterRuntimeServiceServer(s, instrumented)\n```\n\n---\n\n## Part 4: Type Mapping and Vendoring\n\n### Vendoring Location\n\n**containerd's vendored CRI types**:\n```\n/ccb_crossrepo/src/containerd/vendor/k8s.io/cri-api/\n├── pkg/\n│   ├── apis/runtime/v1/\n│   │   ├── api.proto\n│   │   ├── api.pb.go          (Generated message types)\n│   │   ├── api_grpc.pb.go     (Generated gRPC interfaces)\n│   │   └── constants.go\n│ ensuring:\n- Stable interface contract\n- Compatible message schemas\n- Matching gRPC method signatures\n\n### Message Type Flow\n\n```\nKubernetes (canonical):\n    api.proto (source)\n         ↓\n    protoc code generation\n         ↓\n    api.pb.go, api_grpc.pb.go\n         ↓\n    Vendored in Kubernetes repo\n         ↓\n         ↓ (imported as go.mod dependency)\n         ↓\nContainerd:\n    vendor/k8s.io/cri-api/...\n         ↓\n    Import paths: \"k8s.io/cri-api/pkg/apis/runtime/v1\"\n         ↓\n    Used in all RPC handlers\n         ↓\n    Example: runtime.RunPodSandboxRequest -> runtime.RunPodSandboxResponse\n```\n\n### Key Type Categories\n\n1. **Request Messages**: Contain parameters passed by kubelet\n   - `RunPodSandboxRequest` - Sandbox configuration\n   - `CreateContainerRequest` - Container configuration\n   - `ExecSyncRequest` - Command and environment\n\n2. **Response Messages**: Contain results returned to kubelet\n   - `RunPodSandboxResponse` - Sandbox ID\n   - `CreateContainerResponse` - Container ID\n   - `ExecSyncResponse` - Exit code and output\n\n3. **Status Messages**: Describe resource state\n   - `PodSandboxStatus` - Network namespace, IPs, container states\n   - `ContainerStatus` - Process state, resource usage\n   - `RuntimeStatus` - Available services and configurations\n\n4. **Configuration Messages**: Describe resource requirements\n   - `ContainerResources` - CPU, memory, block I/O limits\n   - `LinuxContainerResources` - Linux-specific constraints (cgroups, swap)\n   - `WindowsContainerResources` - Windows-specific constraints\n\n---\n\n## Part 5: Architecture Flow Diagram\n\n```\n┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐\n│                         Kubernetes kubelet Contract\n\n**Interface Definition** (generated in `api_grpc.pb.go`):\n```go\ntype RuntimeServiceServer interface {\n    // Pod Sandbox Management\n    Version(context.Context, *VersionRequest) (*VersionResponse, error)\n    RunPodSandbox(context.Context, *RunPodSandboxRequest) (*RunPodSandboxResponse, error)\n    StopPodSandbox(context.Context, *StopPodSandboxRequest) (*StopPodSandboxResponse, error)\n    RemovePodSandbox(context.Context, *RemovePodSandboxRequest) (*RemovePodSandboxResponse, error)\n\n    // Container Management\n    CreateContainer(context.Context, *CreateContainerRequest) (*CreateContainerResponse, error)\n    StartContainer(context.Context, *StartContainerRequest) (*StartContainerResponse, error)\n\n    // ... 21 more methods\n}\n```\n\n**Containerd Implementation** (`service.go`):\n```go\ntype criService struct {\n    runtime.UnimplementedRuntimeServiceServer  // Provides default error responses\n\n    // Implementation delegates to methods in separate files:\n    // - sandbox_run.go: RunPodSandbox\n    // - sandbox_stop.go: StopPodSandbox\n    // - container_create.go: CreateContainer\n    // etc.\n}\n```\n\n### Key Semantic Guarantees\n\n1. **Idempotency**:\n   - `StopPodSandbox`: Returns success if already stopped\n   - `RemovePodSandbox`: Returns success if already removed\n   - `RemoveImage`: Returns success if already removed\n\n2. **Ordering Requirements**:\n   - Kubelet calls `StopPodSandbox` before `RemovePodSandbox`\n   - Container must exist in sandbox before calling `StartContainer`\n   - Sandbox must be running to create containers\n\n3. **Resource Isolation**:\n   - Each sandbox has isolated network namespace\n   - Containers in sandbox share network namespace\n   - Containers can be isolated via Linux namespaces/cgroups or Windows jobs\n\n---\n\n## Part 7: Important Implementation Patterns\n\n### 1. Metadata Storage Pattern\n\nContainerd maintains metadata stores for both sandboxes and containers:\n\n**Sandbox Store**:\n```go\nsandboxstore.Metadata{\n    ID:             id,           // Unique sandbox ID\n    Name:           name,         // User-friendly name\n    Config:         config,       // Kubernetes PodSandboxConfig\n    RuntimeHandler: runtimeType,  // Which OCI runtime to use\n}\n```\n\n**Container Store**:\n```go\ncontainerstore.Metadata{\n    ID:             id,\n    Name:           name,\n    Config:         config,           // Kubernetes ContainerConfig\n    SandboxID:      parentSandboxID,\n    LogPath:        containerLogPath,\n}\n```\n\n### 2. Name Uniqueness Pattern\n\nBoth sandboxes and containers use `Registrar` for name uniqueness:\n```go\n// Reserve name to prevent conflicts\nif err := c.sandboxNameIndex.Reserve(name, id); err != nil {\n    return nil, fmt.Errorf(\"failed to reserve sandbox name: %w\", err)\n}\n// Release on error\ndefer func() {\n    if retErr != nil {\n        c.sandboxNameIndex.ReleaseByName(name)\n    }\n}()\n```\n\n### 3. OCI Spec Generation Pattern\n\nContainer creation transforms Kubernetes config to OCI spec:\n```\nRunPodSandboxRequest\n    ↓ (transforms)\nOCI Spec (runtime-spec)\n    ↓ (uses)\ncontainerd.Container\n    ↓ (executes)\nOCI Runtime (runc/kata/crun)\n```\n\n### 4. Resource Lease Pattern\n\nContainerd uses leases to track resource lifecycle:\n```go\nls, err := leaseSvc.Create(ctx, leases.WithID(id))\ndefer func() {\n    if err != nil {\n        leaseSvc.Delete(ctx, ls)  // Cleanup on failure\n    }\n}()\n```\n\n### 5. Platform-Specific Implementation Pattern\n\nDifferent implementations for different platforms:\n```\ncontainer_create.go          (Generic logic)\n├── container_create_linux.go    (Linux-specific)\n├── container_create_windows.go  (Windows-specific)\n└── container_create_other.go    (Other platforms)\n```\n\n---\n\n## Part 8: Summary Table\n\n| Component | Location | Purpose |\n|-----------|----------|---------|\n| gRPC Definitions | `staging/src/k8s.io/cri-api/pkg/apis/runtime/v1/api.proto` | Source of truth for CRI contract |\n| Generated Interfaces | `api_grpc.pb.go` | Go interfaces that runtimes implement |\n| Generated Messages | `api.pb.go` | Go structs for request/response types |\n| Plugin Registration | `plugins/cri/cri.go` | Containerd plugin entry point |\n| gRPC Server Setup | `plugins/cri/cri.go:initCRIService()` | Creates and registers service |\n| Core Implementation | `internal/cri/server/service.go` | Main criService struct |\n| Sandbox Operations | `internal/cri/server/sandbox_*.go` | Pod sandbox lifecycle |\n| Container Operations | `internal/cri/server/container_*.go` | Container lifecycle |\n| Image Operations | `internal/cri/server/images/service.go` | Image management |\n| Streaming I/O | `internal/cri/streamingserver/` | Exec/attach/port-forward |\n| Metadata Stores | `internal/cri/store/` | Persistent state |\n| Instrumentation | `internal/cri/instrument/` | Tracing and metrics |\n| Vendored Types | `vendor/k8s.io/cri-api/` | Dependency on Kubernetes types |\n\n---\n\n## Conclusion\n\nThe Kubernetes CRI defines a comprehensive gRPC interface for container runtime operations. Containerd implements this interface through:\n\n1. **Plugin Architecture**: Registering as a containerd gRPC plugin\n2. **Interface Implementation**: Implementing all RuntimeServiceServer and ImageServiceServer methods\n3. **State Management**: Maintaining persistent metadata for sandboxes and containers\n4. **Orchestration**: Coordinating with containerd's core services (snapshots, content, containers)\n5. **Platform Abstraction**: Providing platform-specific implementations while maintaining unified API\n\nThe interface contract is maintained through:\n- **Go module versioning**: Pinning specific `k8s.io/cri-api` versions\n- **Generated code**: Using protobuf code generation for consistency\n- **Semantic guarantees**: Implementing CRI requirements (idempotency, ordering, isolation)\n- **Type safety**: Leveraging Go's type system for compile-time contract verification\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":11,"cache_creation_input_tokens":1099,"cache_read_input_tokens":51327,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":1099},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"0f2cda3a-978d-44d5-870b-d55fa7f69823","uuid":"f2a01f68-4950-4c33-bcda-4137f986c747"}

is a **replace directive**, meaning:\n- Kubernetes maintains CRI API definitions as a staging area\n- The staging source is the canonical location for CRI API definitions\n- Kubernetes can update CRI APIs in lockstep with kubelet changes\n\n**File Structure**:\n```\nstaging/src/k8s.io/cri-api/\n├── pkg/\n│   ├── apis/\n│   │   └── runtime/\n│   │       └── v1/\n│   │           ├── api.proto          # Source definitions\n│   │           ├── api.pb.go          # Generated message types\n│   │           ├── api_grpc.pb.go     # Generated gRPC code\n│   │           └── constants.go       # CRI constants\n│   └── errors/\n│       └── errors.go                  # CRI error definitions\n```\n\n**Key Contract Elements**:\n\n1. **Message Types**: Fully defined in `api.pb.go` with Go struct definitions matching protobuf messages\n2. **gRPC Interfaces**: Defined in `api_grpc.pb.go`\n3. **Constants**:\n   - Error codes (e.g., `RuntimeUnsupported`, `InvalidArgument`)\n   - Log paths, container state constants\n   - Named in `/ccb_crossrepo/src/kubernetes/staging/src/k8s.io/cri-api/pkg/apis/runtime/v1/constants.go`\n\n---\n\n## Part 3: Containerd's CRI Implementation\n\n### Plugin Architecture\n\n**Location**: `/ccb_crossrepo/src/containerd/plugins/cri/`\n\nContainerd implements CRI as a **gRPC plugin** with two main components:\n\n#### 3.1 Plugin Initialization\n\n**File**: `/ccb_crossrepo/src/containerd/plugins/cri/cri.go`\n\n**Plugin Registration**:\n```go\nregistry.Register(&plugin.Registration{\n    Type: plugins.GRPCPlugin,      // Registers as gRPC plugin\n    ID:   \"cri\",\n    Requires: []plugin.Type{\n        plugins.CRIServicePlugin,         // Runtime service dependency\n        plugins.CRIServicePlugin,         // Image service dependency\n        plugins.PodSandboxPlugin,         // Sandbox controller\n        plugins.SandboxControllerPlugin,  // Sandbox management\n        plugins.NRIApiPlugin,             // NRI integration\n        plugins.EventPlugin,              // Event system\n        plugins.ServicePlugin,            // Service registry\n        plugins.LeasePlugin,              // Resource leases\n        plugins.SandboxStorePlugin,       // Sandbox persistence\n        plugins.TransferPlugin,           // Content transfer\n        plugins.WarningPlugin,            // Warning service\n    },\n})\n```\n\n**Initialization Flow**:\n1. Plugin loads runtime service plugin (\"runtime\")\n2. Plugin loads image service plugin (\"images\")\n3. Creates containerd client with in-memory services\n4. Creates CRI gRPC server by calling `server.NewCRIService()`\n5. Wraps server in `criGRPCServer` which implements both `RuntimeServiceServer` and `ImageServiceServer`\n6. Registers servers with gRPC: `runtime.RegisterRuntimeServiceServer()` and `runtime.RegisterImageServiceServer()`\n\n**Key Wrapper** (lines 163-174):\n```go\ntype criGRPCServer struct {\n    runtime.RuntimeServiceServer    // Embedded interface\n    runtime.ImageServiceServer      // Embedded interface\n    io.Closer\n    initializer\n}\n\nfunc (c *criGRPCServer) register(s *grpc.Server) error {\n    instrumented := instrument.NewService(c)\n    runtime.RegisterRuntimeServiceServer(s, instrumented)\n    runtime.RegisterImageServiceServer(s, instrumented)\n    return nil\n}\n```\n\n#### 3.2 Runtime Service Implementation\n\n**Location**: `/ccb_crossrepo/src/containerd/internal/cri/server/`\n\n**Core Service Structure** (`service.go`):\n```go\ntype criService struct {\n    runtime.UnimplementedRuntimeServiceServer\n    runtime.UnimplementedImageServiceServer\n\n    // State management\n    sandboxStore *sandboxstore.Store\n    containerStore *containerstore.Store\n\n    // Clients and plugins\n    client *containerd.Client\n    netPlugin map[string]cni.CNI\n\n    // Execution\n    streamServer streaming.Server\n    eventMonitor *events.EventMonitor\n}\n```\n\n**Inheritance**:\n- Embeds `runtime.UnimplementedRuntimeServiceServer` (from generated protobuf code)\n- This provides stub implementations of all methods\n- Each method is overridden with actual implementation\n\n### Implementation Details by Method Category\n\n#### Pod Sandbox Operations\n\n**RunPodSandbox** (`sandbox_run.go:53`)\n```go\nfunc (c *criService) RunPodSandbox(ctx context.Context, r *runtime.RunPodSandboxRequest)\n    (_ *runtime.RunPodSandboxResponse, retErr error)\n```\n**Flow**:\n1. Generate unique sandbox ID and name\n2. Reserve sandbox name to prevent conflicts\n3. Create containerd lease for resource tracking\n4. Load OCI runtime configuration from request\n5. Contract\n\n**Interface Definition** (generated in `api_grpc.pb.go`):\n```go\ntype RuntimeServiceServer interface {\n    // Pod Sandbox Management\n    Version(context.Context, *VersionRequest) (*VersionResponse, error)\n    RunPodSandbox(context.Context, *RunPodSandboxRequest) (*RunPodSandboxResponse, error)\n    StopPodSandbox(context.Context, *StopPodSandboxRequest) (*StopPodSandboxResponse, error)\n    RemovePodSandbox(context.Context, *RemovePodSandboxRequest) (*RemovePodSandboxResponse, error)\n\n    // Container Management\n    CreateContainer(context.Context, *CreateContainerRequest) (*CreateContainerResponse, error)\n    StartContainer(context.Context, *StartContainerRequest) (*StartContainerResponse, error)\n\n    // ... 21 more methods\n}\n```\n\n**Containerd Implementation** (`service.go`):\n```go\ntype criService struct {\n    runtime.UnimplementedRuntimeServiceServer  // Provides default error responses\n\n    // Implementation delegates to methods in separate files:\n    // - sandbox_run.go: RunPodSandbox\n    // - sandbox_stop.go: StopPodSandbox\n    // - container_create.go: CreateContainer\n    // etc.\n}\n```\n\n### Key Semantic Guarantees\n\n1. **Idempotency**:\n   - `StopPodSandbox`: Returns success if already stopped\n   - `RemovePodSandbox`: Returns success if already removed\n   - `RemoveImage`: Returns success if already removed\n\n2. **Ordering Requirements**:\n   - Kubelet calls `StopPodSandbox` before `RemovePodSandbox`\n   - Container must exist in sandbox before calling `StartContainer`\n   - Sandbox must be running to create containers\n\n3. **Resource Isolation**:\n   - Each sandbox has isolated network namespace\n   - Containers in sandbox share network namespace\n   - Containers can be isolated via Linux namespaces/cgroups or Windows jobs\n\n---\n\n## Part 7: Important Implementation Patterns\n\n### 1. Metadata Storage Pattern\n\nContainerd maintains metadata stores for both sandboxes and containers:\n\n**Sandbox Store**:\n```go\nsandboxstore.Metadata{\n    ID:             id,           // Unique sandbox ID\n    Name:           name,         // User-friendly name\n    Config:         config,       // Kubernetes PodSandboxConfig\n    RuntimeHandler: runtimeType,  // Which OCI runtime to use\n}\n```\n\n**Container Store**:\n```go\ncontainerstore.Metadata{\n    ID:             id,\n    Name:           name,\n    Config:         config,           // Kubernetes ContainerConfig\n    SandboxID:      parentSandboxID,\n    LogPath:        containerLogPath,\n}\n```\n\n### 2. Name Uniqueness Pattern\n\nBoth sandboxes and containers use `Registrar` for name uniqueness:\n```go\n// Reserve name to prevent conflicts\nif err := c.sandboxNameIndex.Reserve(name, id); err != nil {\n    return nil, fmt.Errorf(\"failed to reserve sandbox name: %w\", err)\n}\n// Release on error\ndefer func() {\n    if retErr != nil {\n        c.sandboxNameIndex.ReleaseByName(name)\n    }\n}()\n```\n\n### 3. OCI Spec Generation Pattern\n\nContainer creation transforms Kubernetes config to OCI spec:\n```\nRunPodSandboxRequest\n    ↓ (transforms)\nOCI Spec (runtime-spec)\n    ↓ (uses)\ncontainerd.Container\n    ↓ (executes)\nOCI Runtime (runc/kata/crun)\n```\n\n### 4. Resource Lease Pattern\n\nContainerd uses leases to track resource lifecycle:\n```go\nls, err := leaseSvc.Create(ctx, leases.WithID(id))\ndefer func() {\n    if err != nil {\n        leaseSvc.Delete(ctx, ls)  // Cleanup on failure\n    }\n}()\n```\n\n### 5. Platform-Specific Implementation Pattern\n\nDifferent implementations for different platforms:\n```\ncontainer_create.go          (Generic logic)\n├── container_create_linux.go    (Linux-specific)\n├── container_create_windows.go  (Windows-specific)\n└── container_create_other.go    (Other platforms)\n```\n\n---\n\n## Part 8: Summary Table\n\n| Component | Location | Purpose |\n|-----------|----------|---------|\n| gRPC Definitions | `staging/src/k8s.io/cri-api/pkg/apis/runtime/v1/api.proto` | Source of truth for CRI contract |\n| Generated Interfaces | `api_grpc.pb.go` | Go interfaces that runtimes implement |\n| Generated Messages | `api.pb.go` | Go structs for request/response types |\n| Plugin Registration | `plugins/cri/cri.go` | Containerd plugin entry point |\n| gRPC Server Setup | `plugins/cri/cri.go:initCRIService()` | Creates and registers service |\n| Core Implementation | `internal/cri/server/service.go` | Main criService struct |\n| Sandbox Operations | `internal/cri/server/sandbox_*.go` | Pod sandbox lifecycle |\n| Container Operations | `internal/cri/server/container_*.go` | Container lifecycle |\n| Image Operations | `internal/cri/server/images/service.go` | Image management |\n| Streaming I/O | `internal/cri/streamingserver/` | Exec/attach/port-forward |\n| Metadata Stores | `internal/cri/store/` | Persistent state |\n| Instrumentation | `internal/cri/instrument/` | Tracing and metrics |\n| Vendored Types | `vendor/k8s.io/cri-api/` | Dependency on Kubernetes types |\n\n---\n\n## Conclusion\n\nThe Kubernetes CRI defines a comprehensive gRPC interface for container runtime operations. Containerd implements this interface through:\n\n1. **Plugin Architecture**: Registering as a containerd gRPC plugin\n2. **Interface Implementation**: Implementing all RuntimeServiceServer and ImageServiceServer methods\n3. **State Management**: Maintaining persistent metadata for sandboxes and containers\n4. **Orchestration**: Coordinating with containerd's core services (snapshots, content, containers)\n5. **Platform Abstraction**: Providing platform-specific implementations while maintaining unified API\n\nThe interface contract is maintained through:\n- **Go module versioning**: Pinning specific `k8s.io/cri-api` versions\n- **Generated code**: Using protobuf code generation for consistency\n- **Semantic guarantees**: Implementing CRI requirements (idempotency, ordering, isolation)\n- **Type safety**: Leveraging Go's type system for compile-time contract verification\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
